\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortranscanner_8l_source_l00019}00019 \textcolor{comment}{/* Developer notes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortranscanner_8l_source_l00020}00020 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortranscanner_8l_source_l00021}00021 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/ Consider using startScope(), endScope() functions with  module, program,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortranscanner_8l_source_l00022}00022 \textcolor{comment}{ * subroutine or any other scope in fortran program.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortranscanner_8l_source_l00023}00023 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortranscanner_8l_source_l00024}00024 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/ Symbol yyextra-\/>modifiers (attributes) are collected using SymbolModifiers |= operator during}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortranscanner_8l_source_l00025}00025 \textcolor{comment}{ * substructure parsing. When substructure ends all yyextra-\/>modifiers are applied to actual}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortranscanner_8l_source_l00026}00026 \textcolor{comment}{ * entries in applyModifiers() functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortranscanner_8l_source_l00027}00027 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortranscanner_8l_source_l00028}00028 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/ How case insensitiveness should be handled in code?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortranscanner_8l_source_l00029}00029 \textcolor{comment}{ * On one side we have arg-\/>name and entry-\/>name, on another side modifierMap[name].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortranscanner_8l_source_l00030}00030 \textcolor{comment}{ * In entries and arguments case is the same as in code, in modifier map case is lowered and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortranscanner_8l_source_l00031}00031 \textcolor{comment}{ * then it is compared to lowered entry/argument names.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortranscanner_8l_source_l00032}00032 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortranscanner_8l_source_l00033}00033 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/ Do not like constructs like aa\{BS\} or \{BS\}bb. Should try to handle blank space}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortranscanner_8l_source_l00034}00034 \textcolor{comment}{ * with separate rule?: It seems it is often necessary, because we may parse something like}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortranscanner_8l_source_l00035}00035 \textcolor{comment}{ * "{}functionA"{} or "{}MyInterface"{}. So constructs like '(\string^|[ \(\backslash\)t])interface(\{BS\_\}\{ID\})?/[ \(\backslash\)t\(\backslash\)n]'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortranscanner_8l_source_l00036}00036 \textcolor{comment}{ * are desired.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortranscanner_8l_source_l00037}00037 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortranscanner_8l_source_l00038}00038 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/ Must track yyextra-\/>lineNr when using REJECT, unput() or similar commands.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{src_2fortranscanner_8l_source_l00039}00039 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
